If the player does form such lines of at least five balls of the same color, the balls in those lines disappear, and he gains one turn, i.e. he can move another ball. If not, three new balls are added, and the game continues until the board is full.\r\nFor more challenges and fun, hard mode was introduced, in this mode there will be frozen balls appear after several turns, these balls are unmovable.
